### 21. Field Sport Athlete

- **Domain:** functional | **Axis Bias:** 🔨 | **Gold:** Yes
- **Exercise Pool:** 3270
- **Identity:** Field Sport Athlete is built for transfer. Sprint, jump, cut, decelerate — movement-first. The Functional bias means exercises lean toward athletic transfer — unilateral, standing, ground-based movement. If it does not transfer outside the gym, it does not belong here.

### 35. Explorer / Outdoor Athlete

- **Domain:** specialty | **Axis Bias:** 🔨 | **Gold:** No
- **Exercise Pool:** 3270
- **Identity:** Explorer / Outdoor Athlete is built for a specific craft. Hiking, rucking, trail movement, minimal equipment. The Functional bias means exercises lean toward athletic transfer — unilateral, standing, ground-based movement. Precision in the discipline is the measure.
